add_namespace = fengtian
add_namespace = fngpolitic
add_namespace = fngunif
add_namespace = fngsystem

#################################
### Fengtian Political Events ###
#################################

country_event = { #Rumors incite Regionalist Uproar
	id = fengtian.1
	title = fengtian.1.t
	desc = fengtian.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_official_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.1 option fengtian.1.a"
		name = fengtian.1.a
		add_political_power = -20
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Sentiment
			add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.3 days = 16 }
			set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
		}
	}
}

####Suppress Regionalist Sentiment events###
country_event = { #Protests Continue REPEATING
	id = fengtian.3
	title = fengtian.3.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.3.d4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
		}
	}

	option = { #Unfortunate but necessary
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.3 option fengtian.3.a"
		name = fengtian.3.a
		add_political_power = -15
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				country_event = { id = fengtian.7 days = 25 } # An Offer from the Kenpeitai
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
			}
			country_event = { id = fengtian.3 days = 20 random_days = 25 } # Repeating
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Agent Provocateurs in Action
	id = fengtian.4
	title = fengtian.4.t
	desc = fengtian.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_riot

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Sentiment
			has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
		}
	}

	option = { #Excellent
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.4 option fengtian.4.a"
		name = fengtian.4.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.5 days = 7 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Harbin Riots
	id = fengtian.5
	title = fengtian.5.t
	desc = fengtian.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_official_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good... and bad.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.5 option fengtian.5.a"
		name = fengtian.5.a
		add_political_power = -30
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.6 days = 3 random_days = 3 }
		}
		885 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.5
			}
		}
		886 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
		714 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Mass Arrests Begin
	id = fengtian.6
	title = fengtian.6.t
	desc = fengtian.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_several_prisoners

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good riddance
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.6 option fengtian.6.a"
		name = fengtian.6.a
		add_political_power = 10
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
				}
				country_event = { id = fengtian.8 days = 18 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #An Offer from the Kempeitai
	id = fengtian.7
	title = fengtian.7.t
	desc = fengtian.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_kempeitai

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Take the deal
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.7 option fengtian.7.a"
		name = fengtian.7.a
		unlock_national_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 5 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = -225 } #-45 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_negative_factor
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.8 days = 18 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No thank you
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.7 option fengtian.7.b"
		name = fengtian.7.b
		add_political_power = 10
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -1 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Regionalists suppressed
	id = fengtian.8
	title = fengtian.8.t
	desc = fengtian.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
	}

	option = { #Progress
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.8 option fengtian.8.a"
		name = fengtian.8.a
		add_political_power = 10
		set_country_flag = FNG_regionalists_suppressed
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment }
			remove_ideas = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage }
			remove_ideas = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Picking up the Educational Slack
	id = fengtian.9
	title = fengtian.9.t
	desc = fengtian.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_mantetsu_school

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Close the Schools
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.9 option fengtian.9.a"
		name = fengtian.9.a
		add_political_power = 100
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Educational_Vacuum
			days = 185
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -3 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.12 days = 12 random_days = 36 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #There is no choice
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.9 option fengtian.9.b"
		name = fengtian.9.b
		add_political_power = -30
		add_war_support = -0.03
		set_country_flag = school_open
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = -225 } #-45 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_negative_factor
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.10 days = 150 random_days = 350 }
		}
	}
}

		name = fengtian.10.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				add = ROOT.political_power
				has_political_power < 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.11 days = 53 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #Building Infrastructure in Liaoning
	id = fengtian.13
	title = fengtian.13.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.13.d
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.13.d_jap
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_railway_map

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Chinese Contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.13 option fengtian.13.a"
		name = fengtian.13.a
		set_temp_variable = { CCPOP = 3 }
		FNG_CCPOP = yes
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -3 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian.19 days = 36 }
				}
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian.20 days = 25 }
				}
				50 = { }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Japanese Contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.13 option fengtian.13.b"
		name = fengtian.13.b
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CCPOP = -3 }
		FNG_CCPOP = yes
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 3 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		add_days_remove = {
			decision = FNG_Liaoning_Infrastructure
			days = -100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian.19 days = 36 }
				}
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian.21 days = 25 }
				}
				45 = { }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = -225 } #-45 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_negative_factor
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Imperial Fury
	id = fengtian.22
	title = fengtian.22.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					FNG_JAP_hostile = no
					JAP = {
						is_subject = no
					}
					market_liberal > 0
					market_liberal < 0.05
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
					has_global_flag = japan_punishes_fengtian
				}
				has_global_flag = fengtian_blames_japan
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d_influence_low
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
			}
			market_liberal > 0
			market_liberal < 0.05
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d_fengtian_refuses_food
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
			has_global_flag = japan_punishes_fengtian
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.22.d_fengtian_blames_japan
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = fengtian_blames_japan
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_ultimatum

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		market_liberal < 0.05
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		has_idea = FNG_The_Kwantung_Army
		NOT = {
			has_idea = FNG_Japanese_Aid_Cut
			has_idea_with_trait = FNG_kwantung_liaison
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #A hard lesson
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.22 option fengtian.22.a"
		name = fengtian.22.a
		add_political_power = -50
		FNG_japan_cuts_aid = yes
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 10 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 85
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_game_rule = { rule = FNG_path option = FNG_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Expel their officers in retaliation!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.22 option fengtian.22.b"
		name = fengtian.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = JAP
					ratio < 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = FNG_conference_begun
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FNG_path option = FNG_PATH_MARLIB }
			}
		}
		country_event = fengtian.76
		custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_expel_japanese_officers_tooltip
	}
}

				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Chosabu Intelligence 1
	id = fengtian.67
	title = fengtian.67.t
	desc = fengtian.67.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_science

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.67 option fengtian.67.a"
		name = fengtian.67.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dlc_lar = yes
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fengtian.67.t
				bonus = 0.66
				uses = 1
				category = decryption_tech
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_intelligence_agency = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_crypto_strength
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_crypto_strength
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_decryption_boost
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_crypto_strength
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost
						}
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_training_centers
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_training_centers
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_intelligence_agency = yes
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_decryption_boost
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = fengtian.77
	title = fengtian.77.t

	desc = {
		text = fengtian.77.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_breakaway } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.77.d_breakaway
		trigger = { has_country_flag = FNG_breakaway }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_ultimatum

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;JAP WAR ON FNG;[GetDateText]"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = FNG_relations_JAP_broke
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			JAP = {
				every_owned_state = {
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = { is_ally_with = FNG }
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FNG
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FNG
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FNG
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = FNG
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Zhongua Mingguo Wansui!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.77 option fengtian.77.a"
		name = fengtian.77.a
		JAP = {
			clear_JAP_FNG_hostile_AI = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = FNG_breakaway
		add_political_power = 200
		FNG_CA_remove = yes
		FNG_mantetsu_collapse = yes
	}
}

	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_ultimatum

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #We can do nothing
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.78 option fengtian.78.a"
		name = fengtian.78.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 55
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FNG_path option = FNG_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		add_ideas = FNG_The_Kwantung_Army
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.78 option fengtian.78.b"
		name = fengtian.78.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FNG_path option = FNG_PATH_MARLIB }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = FNG_relations_JAP_broke
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		JAP = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FNG
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = annex_everything
		}
		FNG_CA_remove = yes
		FNG_mantetsu_collapse = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Escalate the Propaganda War
	id = fengtian.91
	title = fengtian.91.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.91.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
				FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.91.d_mantetsu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
				FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_ambassador_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.91 option fengtian.91.a"
		name = fengtian.91.a
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes }
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes }
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_medium = yes }
			add_political_power = 30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_low = yes }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_none = yes }
			add_political_power = 80
		}
	}
}

	}

	desc = {

		trigger = { FNG = { is_subject = no } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.136.d.puppeted
		trigger = { FNG = { is_subject = yes } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_warlord_battle

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = FNG }
			FNG = { is_subject = yes }
		}
		can_declare_war_on = FROM
		is_faction_leader = yes
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china }
	}

	option = { #Zhang is on his own
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.136 option fengtian.136.a"
		name = fengtian.136.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.136 option fengtian.136.b"
		name = fengtian.136.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				surrender_progress > 0.15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FNG = { is_subject = yes } }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FNG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 716 } } #Shenyang
			create_wargoal = {
				target = var:716.owner
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = var:885.owner
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_country_flag = soldierly_discipline_enabled
					has_country_flag = FNG_completed_fortress_manchuria_decision
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_impressed_prince
			add_political_power = 20
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = prince_impress_level
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = soldierly_discipline_enabled
					has_country_flag = FNG_completed_fortress_manchuria_decision
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prince_shot
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.149 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = prince_shot
				}
				has_completed_focus = FNG_Establish_the_Jinzhou_Industrial_Zone
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.145 days = 5 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = prince_shot
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Establish_the_Jinzhou_Industrial_Zone
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.146 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #It is safest to end the visit here
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.144 option fengtian.144.b"
		name = fengtian.144.b
		clr_country_flag = FNG_prince_visit
		hidden_effect = { FNG_close_FNG_Preparing_For_The_Princes_Visit = yes }
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -3 }
		FNG_CAPOP = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Tang Yulin Tempts Fate
	id = fengtian.158
	title = fengtian.158.t
	desc = fengtian.158.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_warlord_battle

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FNG_tang_yulin = { has_advisor_role = political_advisor }
		can_declare_war_on = MON
		is_neighbor_of = MON
		MON = {
			owns_state = 612
			controls_state = 612
		}
	}

	option = { #We must strike before they do!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.158 option fengtian.158.a"
		name = fengtian.158.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = QIE #too risky
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					MON = { is_in_faction_with = RUS } #do not commit suicide
					MON = { is_guaranteed_by = RUS }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ROOT_is_threatened = yes
					MON = { default_attack_AI_trigger_FROM = yes }
					MON = { dont_start_major_faction_wars = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = MON
			type = take_state
			generator = { 612 }
		}
		add_manpower = -1000
		set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = 3 }
		FNG_ZCPOP = yes
		MON = { country_event = fengtian.159 }
	}

	option = { #Tang has done enough damage already!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.158 option fengtian.158.b"
		name = fengtian.158.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = -30
		add_manpower = -1000
		set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
		FNG_ZCPOP = yes
		MON = { country_event = fengtian.160 }
	}

	option = { #Maybe things will de-escalate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.158 option fengtian.158.c"
		name = fengtian.158.c
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		add_manpower = -5000
		MON = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.161 days = 2 }
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.162 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Zongchang and Anqing prevent war hidden prep event, triggered by lepcollapse.26
	id = fengtian.212
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_started
		SQI = { #Zongchang controls at least one 5P state
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { state = 597 } #jinan west shandong
					NOT = { state = 1065 } #jiaodong north shandong
					NOT = { state = 1064 } #linyi south shandong
				}
				FNG = { add_to_array = { SQI_owned_league_states = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #checks if a proper state exists, if it does than indeed sqi owns 5P states
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = SQI_owned_league_states
					is_owned_by = SQI
				}
			}

			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = SQI_owned_league_states
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { state = 1047 }
						NOT = { state = 598 }
						NOT = { state = 1075 }
					}
					FNG = { add_to_array = { SQI_owned_crit_anq_states = PREV } }
				}
				else = {
					FNG = { add_to_array = { SQI_owned_jiangsu_states = PREV } }
				}
			}

			if = { #checks if a proper state exis, if yes than sqi owns 5P states crit by ANQ
				limit = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = SQI_owned_crit_anq_states
						is_owned_by = SQI
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_controls_5p_crit_state
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_jiangsu
				SQI = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								controls_state = 1047
								controls_state = 598
								controls_state = 1075
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 1047 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 1047 } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 598 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 598 } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 1075 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 1075 } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong

		}

		country_event = { id = fengtian.213 days = 1 }
	}
}

				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_p1_anqno }
					country_event = { id = fengtian.222 days = 1 }
				}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin's Proposal Accepted
	id = fengtian.221
	title = fengtian.221.t
	desc = fengtian.221.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.221 option fengtian.221.a"
		name = fengtian.221.a
		set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_paccepted
		ANQ = {
			country_event = { id = anq.132 days = 1 }
		}
		SQI = {
			country_event = { id = shandong.36 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_lep_beat_chi } }
			country_event = { id = fengtian.225 days = 14 }
			ANQ = {
				country_event = { id = anq.136 days = 11 }
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.40 days = 11 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong }
			}
			ANQ = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = FNG.SQI_owned_league_states
					transfer_state = v
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_keepjiangsu
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_jiangsu }
			}
			ANQ = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = FNG.SQI_owned_crit_anq_states
					transfer_state = v
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu } }
				SQI = {
					transfer_state = 1047
					transfer_state = 598
					transfer_state = 1075
				}
			}
			else = {
				SQI = {
					for_each_loop = {
						array = FNG.SQI_nonowned_jiangsu_states
						transfer_state = v
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin's Proposal Rejected
	id = fengtian.222
	title = fengtian.222.t
	desc = fengtian.222.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.222 option fengtian.222.a"
		name = fengtian.222.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong
			}
			#shandong only shandong, anq offers but fengtian doesnt
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqall5p }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong }
			}
			#all situations but shandong having only shandong
			#if they have critical part, they keep all of jiangsu
			#if they have jiangsu parts, they keep those parts
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_controls_5p_crit_state
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_cedenonjiangsu
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqiwantjiangsu }
			}
			#shandong part jiangsu, doesnt need rest jiangsu
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong
			}
			#shandong only shandong, if anq is willing get all jiangsu, if not only xuhai potent
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_getxuhai
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_everything
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqikeepall }
			}
			#shandong controls a crit state, but is actually willing to give up
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			ANQ = {
				country_event = { id = anq.131 days = 1 }
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = shandong.35 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Fengtian Presents a Compromise
	id = fengtian.229
	title = fengtian.229.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.229.d1split
		trigger = {
			tag = ANQ
			FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_split }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.229.d1specrzhang
		trigger = {
			tag = ANQ
			FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.229.d1specrchen
		trigger = {
			tag = ANQ
			FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrchen }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.229.d2split
		trigger = {
			tag = SQI
			FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_split }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.229.d2specrzhang
		trigger = {
			tag = SQI
			FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.229.d2specrchen
		trigger = {
			tag = SQI
			FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrchen }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.229 option fengtian.229.a"
		name = fengtian.229.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					tag = ANQ
					FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang }
				}
				AND = {
					tag = SQI
					FNG = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang
							has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrchen
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				tag = ANQ
				FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				tag = SQI
				FNG = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrchen
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_ANQ }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_SQI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_NOONE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ANQ }
				FNG = {
					set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqyes
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqiyes }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.233 days = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqino }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.234 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				FNG = {
					set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqiyes
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqyes }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.233 days = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqno }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.234 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.229 option fengtian.229.b"
		name = fengtian.229.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				tag = ANQ
				FNG = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				tag = SQI
				FNG = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang
						has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrchen
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_PEACE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ANQ }
				FNG = {
					set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqno
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqiyes }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.234 days = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqino }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.234 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}

						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqno }
						country_event = { id = fengtian.234 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Compromise is Accepted
	id = fengtian.233
	title = fengtian.233.t
	desc = fengtian.233.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.233 option fengtian.233.a"
		name = fengtian.233.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = FNG }
			give_guarantee = SQI
			if = {
				limit = { 1047 = { is_controlled_by = SQI } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 1047 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 598 = { is_controlled_by = SQI } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 598 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 1075 = { is_controlled_by = SQI } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 1075 }
			}

			ANQ = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.233 days = 1 }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = anq.64 days = 4 }
					remove_targeted_decision = { decision = ANQ_attack_SQI target = SQI }
				}
				set_country_flag = ANQ_sqi_is_ally

				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SQI state = 1047 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SQI state = 598 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SQI state = 1075 }
			}
			SQI = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.233 days = 1 }
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_targeted_decision = { decision = SQI_intervene_southeast target = ANQ }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 1047.building_level@industrial_complex }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 598.building_level@industrial_complex }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 1075.building_level@industrial_complex }

				set_temp_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 1047.building_level@arms_factory }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 598.building_level@arms_factory }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 1075.building_level@arms_factory }

				add_offsite_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories
				}
				add_offsite_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = SQI_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories
				}
			}

			1047 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			598 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			1075 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			597 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SQI_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			set_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_success
			hidden_effect = { country_event = lepcollapse.29 }
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqall5p
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqgivejiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqtheykeepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_anqthreatzhang
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_first_demands_heard
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_cedenonjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_getxuhai
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_p1_anqno
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_p1_anqyes
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_p1_sqino
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_p1_sqiyes
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_everything
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_getjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_inshandong
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_shd_keepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_controls_5p_crit_state
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_notall_jiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_jiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqi_only_shandong
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqikeepall
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqikeepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc_sqiwantjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqno
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqyes
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrchen
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_specrzhang
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_split
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqino
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_sqiyes
		}

		}
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.234 option fengtian.234.b"
		name = fengtian.234.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50

				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqsqi_warc2_anqno }

			}

		name = fengtian.239.a
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = QIE
			}
			set_country_flag = FNG_shenyang_anq_only
			country_event = { id = fngshen.1 random_hours = 12 days = 1 }
			ANQ = {
				clr_country_flag = ANQ_feng_aid_undecided
				set_country_flag = ANQ_no_reconstruction_aid
			}
		}
		else = {
			ANQ = { #anqing will ask reconstruction
				country_event = { id = anq.161 days = 5 }
			}
		}
		give_guarantee = ANQ
	}
}

			base = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FNG_path option = FNG_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_yuting_chance_1 = ROOT.party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_yuting_chance_1 = 10 }
				add = FNG_yuting_chance_1
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_yuting_chance_2 = FNG.FNG_legitimacy_level }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_yuting_chance_2 = -1 }
				add = FNG_yuting_chance_2
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		retire_character = FNG_zhang_zuolin
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.299 random_hours = 24 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Yuting Takes Over
	id = fengtian.299
	title = fengtian.299.t
	desc = fengtian.299.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_conscription

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.299 option fengtian.299.a"
		name = fengtian.299.a
		#save popularities
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_totalist = FNG.party_popularity_100@totalist }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_syndicalist = FNG.party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_radical_socialist = FNG.party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_social_democrat = FNG.party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_social_liberal = FNG.party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_market_liberal = FNG.party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_social_conservative = FNG.party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_authoritarian_democrat = FNG.party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_paternal_autocrat = FNG.party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_national_populist = FNG.party_popularity_100@national_populist }

		#calculate marlib popularity
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_totalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_syndicalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_radical_socialist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_social_democrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_social_liberal }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_social_conservative }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_authoritarian_democrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_marlib_final_popularity = FNG_national_populist }

		set_cosmetic_tag = FNG_JAP
		set_global_flag = FNG_projapan
		clr_country_flag = FNG_communications_clique_active
		clr_country_flag = FNG_recovery_league_active
		clr_country_flag = FNG_zhang_clique_active

		remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = FNG_favor_concordia_association }
		remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = FNG_favor_communications_clique }
		remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = FNG_favor_recovery_league }
		remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = FNG_favor_zhang_clique }

		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.301 hours = 8 }
				country_event = { id = fengtian.300 days = 5 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			JAP = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = kr_default_puppet
					end_wars = no
				}
				country_event = { id = fengtian.300 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		FNG_yang_yuting = { promote_leader = yes }
		retire_character = FNG_zhang_xueliang
		retire_character = FNG_wu_junsheng
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = FNG_factionalism_modifier }
			default_party_popularity_PP_gain = yes
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = FNG_totalist
				syndicalist = FNG_syndicalist
				radical_socialist = FNG_radical_socialist
				social_democrat = FNG_social_democrat
				social_liberal = FNG_social_liberal
				market_liberal = FNG_marlib_final_popularity
				social_conservative = FNG_social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = FNG_authoritarian_democrat
				paternal_autocrat = 0
				national_populist = FNG_national_populist
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			FNG_recalculate_mantetsu_effects = yes
			unlock_national_focus = FNG_The_Question_of_the_Presidency
			country_event = { id = fengtian.308 days = 2 } #Restoring Order to Manchuria
			news_event = worldnews.475
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { china_is_potential_government = yes }
				country_event = fengtian.3000
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

				limit = {
					is_valid_peace_target = yes
					surrender_progress > 0.85

			}
		}
	}

		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.310 option fengtian.310.a"
		name = fengtian.310.a
		add_political_power = 15
		add_manpower = -15000
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # Arisaka Type 38 ~1918
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = -300
			producer = JAP
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1934
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			amount = -50
			producer = JAP
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe
				amount = -3
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = small_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = -6
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		FNG = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.311 hours = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 3 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
	}

	option = { #Provide weapons and reconnaissance (Reduces expedition cost for FNG)
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian.310 option fengtian.310.b"
		name = fengtian.310.b
		add_political_power = 5
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # Arisaka Type 38 ~1918
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -100
			producer = JAP
		}

			limit = { has_design_based_on = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe
				amount = -3
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = small_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = -6
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_boosted_expedition_jap
		FNG = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian.314 hours = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 1 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}

	}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_2
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_1

							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_2
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_2
						}
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_2
				#break = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = fngsystem.7 days = 20 random_days = 5 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Radar

country_event = { #Encryption Codes Leaked!
	id = fngpolitic.15
	title = fngpolitic.15.t
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.15.d_Ruan
		trigger = {
			FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_character = event_target:leaker }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.15.d_Wang
		trigger = {
			FNG_wang_yintai = { is_character = event_target:leaker }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.15.d_Tang
		trigger = {
			FNG_tang_yulin = { is_character = event_target:leaker }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_harbin

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government = authoritarian_democrat
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = FNG_encryption_codes_leaked
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { save_event_target_as = leaker }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_wang_yintai = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			FNG_wang_yintai = { save_event_target_as = leaker }
		}
		else = {
			FNG_tang_yulin = { save_event_target_as = leaker }
		}
	}

	option = { #Damn!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fngpolitic.15 option fngpolitic.15.a"
		name = fngpolitic.15.a
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		add_political_power = -20
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Intel_Leak
			days = 60
		}
		if = { #It's Ruan Zhenduo
			limit = { FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 3 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		else_if = { #It's Wang Yintai
			limit = { FNG_wang_yintai = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = -3 }
			FNG_RLPOP = yes
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 1 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		else = { #It's Tang Yulin
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 1 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { JAP = { is_ai = no } }
				JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { QIE = { is_ai = no } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						is_ai = no
					}
					country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { LEC = { is_ai = no } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china
								JAP = { is_faction_leader = no }
							}
						}
						JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								NOT = { country_exists = LEC }
								LEC = { is_in_faction = yes }
								LEC = { is_subject = yes }
							}
						}
						LEC = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_war = no
						}
						random_enemy_country = {
							limit = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT }
							country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_war = yes
						}
						random_other_country = {
							limit = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT }
							country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Remove him from office!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fngpolitic.15 option fngpolitic.15.b"
		name = fngpolitic.15.b
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Intel_Leak
			days = 60
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = -3 }
			FNG_CAPOP = yes
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = 3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
			deactivate_advisor = FNG_ruan_zhenduo_political_advisor
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_japan_dislike
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_wang_yintai = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = -3 }
			FNG_RLPOP = yes
			deactivate_advisor = FNG_wang_yintai
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { JAP = { is_ai = no } }
				JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { QIE = { is_ai = no } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						is_ai = no
					}
					country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { LEC = { is_ai = no } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china
								JAP = { is_faction_leader = no }
							}
						}
						JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								NOT = { country_exists = LEC }
								LEC = { is_in_faction = yes }
								LEC = { is_subject = yes }
							}
						}
						LEC = { country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 } }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_war = no
						}
						random_enemy_country = {
							limit = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT }
							country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_war = yes
						}
						random_other_country = {
							limit = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT }
							country_event = { id = fengtian.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Protests
	id = fngpolitic.28

	title = {
		text = fngpolitic.28.t.minor
		trigger = {
			NOT = { FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = fngpolitic.28.t.major
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.28.d.minor
		trigger = {
			NOT = { FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.28.d.major
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value
			value < 6
		}
		OR = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value
					value = 5
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian.321 hours = 66 } #An End to the Protests
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fngpolitic.28 option fngpolitic.28.a"
		name = fngpolitic.28.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes }
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = FNG_projapan
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value value = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fngpolitic.28 option fngpolitic.28.a"
		name = fngpolitic.28.a
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = FNG_projapan
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value value = 1 }
		}
	}
}
